game_balance_tech_stage_1a = {
allow = {
 has_country_flag = impossible
 OR = {
 AND = {
  date = 1936.1.1
  game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 0
  NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 1 }
 }
 AND = {
  date = 1936.3.30
  game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 1
  NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 2 }
 }
 AND = {
  date = 1936.7.30
  game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 2
  NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 3 }
 }
 AND = {
  date = 1936.11.30
  game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 3
  NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 4 }
 }
 AND = {
  date = 1937.3.30
  game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 4
  NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 5 }
 }
 AND = {
  date = 1937.7.30
  game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 5
  NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 6 }
 }
 AND = {
  date = 1937.11.30
  game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 6
  NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 7 }
 }
 AND = {
  date = 1938.3.30
  game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 7
  NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 8 }
 }
 AND = {
  date = 1938.7.30
  game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 8
  NOT = { game_balance_tech_stage_1a = 9 }
 }
 not = { year = 1939 }
 }
}
